This file contains the 300 dpi bitmap fonts for the GreekSyntax and
GreekTimes font families. The bitmap fonts are required only if the
PostScript printer dirver PSPrinter is used in Oberon for Windows. To install
the font files, start Oberon for Windows, open this text file with Edit.Open
and change the current directory to be the fonts directory (e.g.
c:\oberon\fonts if your Oberon for Windows is installed in c:\oberon.) Then,
execute the command AsciiCoder.DecodeFiles written below to unpack the font
files.

AsciiCoder.DecodeFiles % GreekSyntax10.Pr3.Fnt GreekSyntax12.Pr3.Fnt GreekSyntax14.Pr3.Fnt GreekSyntax16.Pr3.Fnt GreekSyntax20.Pr3.Fnt GreekSyntax24.Pr3.Fnt GreekTimes10.Pr3.Fnt GreekTimes12.Pr3.Fnt GreekTimes14.Pr3.Fnt GreekTimes16.Pr3.Fnt GreekTimes20.Pr3.Fnt GreekTimes24.Pr3.Fnt ~
